+    // Helper untuk mengonversi Google Drive file URL menjadi thumbnail image URL
+    function getImageUrl(val) {
+      if (!val) return '';
+      if (val.indexOf('data:image/') === 0) {
+        return val;
+      }
+      if (val.indexOf('http') === 0) {
+        const match = val.match(/(?:id=|\/d\/)([a-zA-Z0-9-_]{25,50})/);
+        if (match && match[1]) {
+          return `https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=${match[1]}&sz=w300`;
+        }
+        return val;
+      }
+      return '';
+    }

-    const exportToCSV = (dataList, filename) => {
+    async function uploadImageToSupabaseStorage(base64Str, nopol, fieldName) {
+      if (!base64Str) return '';
+      const cleanBase64 = String(base64Str).trim();
+      
+      // If it's already a URL, don't upload again
+      if (cleanBase64.startsWith('http://') || cleanBase64.startsWith('https://')) {
+        return cleanBase64;
+      }
+      
+      // If it doesn't look like base64, return as is
+      if (!cleanBase64.startsWith('data:')) {
+        return cleanBase64;
+      }
+      
+      try {
+        const matches = cleanBase64.match(/^data:([a-zA-Z0-9]+\/[a-zA-Z0-9-.+]+);base64,(.+)$/);
+        if (!matches || matches.length !== 3) {
+          return cleanBase64;
+        }
+        
+        const contentType = matches[1];
+        const b64Data = matches[2];
+        
+        const byteCharacters = atob(b64Data);
+        const byteNumbers = new Array(byteCharacters.length);
+        for (let i = 0; i < byteCharacters.length; i++) {
+          byteNumbers[i] = byteCharacters.charCodeAt(i);
+        }
+        const byteArray = new Uint8Array(byteNumbers);
+        const blob = new Blob([byteArray], { type: contentType });
+        
+        // Generate filename
+        const ext = contentType.split('/')[1] || 'jpg';
+        const cleanNopol = String(nopol || 'unknown').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_').toUpperCase();
+        const filename = `${cleanNopol}_${fieldName}_${Date.now()}.${ext}`;
+        
+        // Upload to Supabase Storage
+        const { data, error } = await supabaseClient.storage
+          .from('gps-images')
+          .upload(filename, blob, {
+            contentType: contentType,
+            upsert: true
+          });
+          
+        if (error) {
+          console.error("Storage upload error:", error);
+          throw error;
+        }
+        
+        // Get public URL
+        const { data: urlData } = supabaseClient.storage
+          .from('gps-images')
+          .getPublicUrl(filename);
+          
+        return urlData.publicUrl;
+      } catch (err) {
+        console.error("Failed to upload base64 to Supabase Storage:", err);
+        return cleanBase64; // Fallback
+      }
+    }
+

+    function ProgressMonitoringView({ units, isMobile }) {
+      const [q, setQ] = useState('');
+      const [loc, setLoc] = useState('');
+      const [poolF, setPoolF] = useState('');
+      const [st, setSt] = useState('');
+      const [merkF, setMerkF] = useState('');
+      const [assetTypeF, setAssetTypeF] = useState('');
+      const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
+      const PAGE_LIMIT = 50;
+
+      const uniqueMerks = useMemo(() => {
+        return [...new Set(units.map(u => u.merk).filter(Boolean))].sort();
+      }, [units]);
+
+      const uniqueAssetTypes = useMemo(() => {
+        return [...new Set(units.map(u => u.assetType).filter(Boolean))].sort();
+      }, [units]);
+
+      const workflowStages = [
+        { name: 'UNPLAN', label: 'Unplan' },
+        { name: 'PLAN', label: 'Plan' },
+        { name: 'INSTALLATION', label: 'Installing' },
+        { name: 'TEKNISI_SUBMITTED', label: 'Teknisi' },
+        { name: 'PIC_VERIFIED', label: 'PIC' },
+        { name: 'IT_VERIFIED', label: 'IT' },
+        { name: 'CMT', label: 'CMT' },
+        { name: 'COMPLETED', label: 'Done' }
+      ];
+
+      const getUnitCurrentStage = (u) => {
+        if (u.statusPlan === 'UNPLAN') return 'UNPLAN';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'ON PROGRESS') return 'INSTALLATION';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'TEKNISI SUBMITTED') return 'TEKNISI_SUBMITTED';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'PIC VERIFIED') return 'PIC_VERIFIED';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'IT VERIFIED') return 'IT_VERIFIED';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'CMT PENDING') return 'CMT';
+        if (u.statusPasang === 'DONE') return 'COMPLETED';
+        return 'PLAN';
+      };
+
+      const getStageStatus = (currentStage, stageName) => {
+        const order = ['UNPLAN', 'PLAN', 'INSTALLATION', 'TEKNISI_SUBMITTED', 'PIC_VERIFIED', 'IT_VERIFIED', 'CMT', 'COMPLETED'];
+        const currentIndex = order.indexOf(currentStage);
+        const stageNameIndex = order.indexOf(stageName);
+        if (currentIndex === stageNameIndex) return 'active';
+        if (stageNameIndex < currentIndex) return 'past';
+        return 'future';
+      };
+
+      const renderStageCell = (currentStage, stageName) => {
+        const status = getStageStatus(currentStage, stageName);
+        
+        if (status === 'active') {
+          let colorClass = 'progress-dot active';
+          if (currentStage === 'INSTALLATION' || currentStage === 'TEKNISI_SUBMITTED') {
+            colorClass = 'progress-dot warning animate-pulse';
+          } else if (currentStage === 'COMPLETED') {
+            colorClass = 'progress-dot success';
+          } else {
+            colorClass = 'progress-dot primary animate-pulse';
+          }
+          return (
+            <span className={colorClass} title={`Sedang di tahap: ${stageName}`} />
+          );
+        }
+        if (status === 'past') {
+          return (
+            <span className="progress-dot past" title={`Selesai: ${stageName}`} />
+          );
+        }
+        return (
+          <span className="progress-dot future" title={`Antrean: ${stageName}`} />
+        );
+      };
+
+      const getLastActivityNote = (u) => {
+        const stage = getUnitCurrentStage(u);
+        switch (stage) {
+          case 'UNPLAN':
+            return { activity: 'Belum Plan', notes: 'Menunggu pembuatan jadwal pemasangan.' };
+          case 'PLAN':
+            return { activity: 'Jadwal Dibuat', notes: `Rencana pasang: ${u.planDate} di ${u.lokasiPasang || '—'}.` };
+          case 'INSTALLATION':
+            return { activity: 'Instalasi Lapangan', notes: `Sedang dipasang oleh ${u.teknisiPelaksana || 'Teknisi'}.` };
+          case 'TEKNISI_SUBMITTED':

+          case 'PIC_VERIFIED':
+            return { activity: 'Verifikasi IT', notes: 'Fisik OK. Menunggu verifikasi integrasi IT Puninar.' };
+          case 'IT_VERIFIED':
+            return { activity: 'Verifikasi CMT', notes: 'Integrasi data OK. Menunggu verifikasi final CMT (Terminasi).' };
+          case 'COMPLETED':
+            return { activity: 'Migrasi Selesai', notes: 'Unit aktif penuh dan vendor lama sudah diterminasi.' };
+          default:
+            return { activity: 'Update Data', notes: u.updatedAt ? `Pembaruan terakhir pada ${u.updatedAt}` : 'Data terdaftar.' };
+        }
+      };

+      const filtered = useMemo(() => {
+        return units.filter(u => 
+          (!q || u.nopol.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase())) &&
+          (!loc || u.location === loc) &&

+          (!assetTypeF || u.assetType === assetTypeF)
+        );
+      }, [units, q, loc, poolF, st, merkF, assetTypeF]);
+
+      const total = Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_LIMIT);
+      const slice = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_LIMIT, page * PAGE_LIMIT);
+
+      return (
+        <div className="fade-in">
+          <div className="role-banner verifikasi">
+            <i className="ti ti-activity" style={{ fontSize: 18 }}></i>

+          </div>
+
+          <FilterRow>

+                <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 48, color: 'var(--text-tertiary)', background: 'var(--bg-card)', borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)', border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  <i className="bi bi-list-check" style={{ fontSize: 32, display: 'block', marginBottom: 10, color: 'var(--text-tertiary)' }}></i>
+                  Tidak ada unit berstatus PIC VERIFIED yang membutuhkan verifikasi IT.
+                </div>
+              ) : isMobile ? (
+                <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 12, marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  {slice.map(u => (
+                    <div key={u.id} className="mobile-unit-card" style={{ padding: 14 }}>
+                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
+                        <strong style={{ fontSize: 15 }}>{u.nopol}</strong>
+                        <Badge val={u.statusPasang} />
+                      </div>
+                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', marginTop: 6 }}>
+                        <div>Site: {u.location} • Pool: {u.pool}</div>
+                        <div>PIC Lapangan: <strong>{u.picLapangan || '—'}</strong></div>
+                      </div>
+                      <button className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" style={{ width: '100%', marginTop: 12, justifyContent: 'center' }} onClick={() => { setEditId(u.id); setItCekAplikasi('OK'); setItFotoIntegrasi(''); setItFotoAbnormality(''); }}>
+                        <i className="bi bi-clipboard-check"></i> Mulai Verifikasi IT
+                      </button>
                     </div>
-
-                    <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: 8, fontSize: 11, marginTop: 8 }}>
-                      <div>GPS: <Badge val={u.gps} /></div>
-                      <div>Buzzer: <Badge val={u.buzzer} /></div>
-                      <div>SOS: <Badge val={u.sos} /></div>
-                      <div>Wing: <Badge val={u.sensorWing} /></div>
+                  ))}
+                </div>
+              ) : (
+                <div className="table-container" style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  <table className="data-table">
+                    <thead>
+                      <tr>
+                        <th>#</th>
+                        <th>NOPOL</th>
+                        <th>LOCATION</th>
+                        <th>PIC LAPANGAN</th>
+                        <th>TEKNISI</th>
+                        <th>SN GPS BARU</th>
+                        <th>AKSI</th>
+                      </tr>
+                    </thead>
+                    <tbody>
+                      {slice.map((u, i) => (
+                        <tr key={u.id}>
+                          <td className="text-muted">{(page - 1) * PAGE_LIMIT + i + 1}</td>
+                          <td><strong>{u.nopol}</strong></td>
+                          <td>{u.location}</td>
+                          <td>{u.picLapangan || '—'}</td>
+                          <td>{u.teknisiPelaksana || '—'}</td>
+                          <td><code>{u.gpsSerialBaru || '—'}</code></td>
+                          <td>
+                            <button className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onClick={() => { setEditId(u.id); setItCekAplikasi('OK'); setItFotoIntegrasi(''); setItFotoAbnormality(''); }}>
+                              <i className="bi bi-clipboard-check"></i> Verifikasi IT
+                            </button>
+                          </td>
+                        </tr>
+                      ))}
+                    </tbody>
+                  </table>
+                </div>
+              )}
+              {filtered.length > 0 && <Pager page={page} total={total} onChange={p => setPage(p)} />}
+            </>
+          ) : (
+            <div className="panel-card fade-in" style={{ padding: 20 }}>
+              <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 16, paddingBottom: 12, borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-color)' }}>
+                <span style={{ fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 15 }}>Form Verifikasi IT: {editingUnit.nopol}</span>
+                <button className="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onClick={() => setEditId(null)}>Batal</button>
+              </div>
+
+              <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: isMobile ? '1fr' : '1.2fr 1fr', gap: 24 }}>
+                <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 16 }}>
+                  <div style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)', borderRadius: 8, padding: 14, border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', fontSize: 12 }}>
+                    <h4 style={{ margin: '0 0 10px 0', fontSize: 13, borderBottom: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05)', paddingBottom: 6 }}>Rangkuman Lapangan</h4>
+                    <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: 10 }}>
+                      <div>Nopol: <strong>{editingUnit.nopol}</strong></div>
+                      <div>Tipe: <strong>{editingUnit.merk} {editingUnit.assetType}</strong></div>
+                      <div>GPS Baru: <code>{editingUnit.gpsSerialBaru}</code></div>
+                      <div>Teknisi: <strong>{editingUnit.teknisiPelaksana}</strong></div>
+                      <div>PIC Lapangan: <strong>{editingUnit.picLapangan}</strong></div>
+                      <div>Cek Fisik GPS Lama: <Badge val={editingUnit.picCekFisikLama} /></div>
+                      <div>Cek Fisik GPS Baru: <Badge val={editingUnit.picCekFisikBaru} /></div>
+                      <div>Cek Fitur Lapangan: <Badge val={editingUnit.picCekFitur} /></div>
                     </div>
-
-                    <div style={{ borderTop: '1px solid var(--border-color)', paddingTop: 10, marginTop: 10 }}>
-                      {isEdit ? (
-                        <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 10 }}>
-                          <div className="input-group">
-                            <label className="input-label" style={{ fontSize: 10 }}>STATUS SISTEM</label>
-                            <select value={editData.statusSystem || ''} onChange={e => setEditData(d => ({ ...d, statusSystem: e.target.value }))} className="filter-select" style={{ width: '100%', height: 36 }}>
-                              <option value="">— Pilih —</option>
-                              {SYS_OPTS.map(o => <option key={o} value={o}>{o}</option>)}
-                            </select>
-                          </div>
-                          <div className="input-group">
-                            <label className="input-label" style={{ fontSize: 10 }}>SUSPEND EASYGO</label>
-                            <select value={editData.statusSuspend || ''} onChange={e => setEditData(d => ({ ...d, statusSuspend: e.target.value }))} className="filter-select" style={{ width: '100%', height: 36 }}>
-                              <option value="">— Pilih —</option>
-                              {SUSPEND_OPTS.map(o => <option key={o} value={o}>{o}</option>)}
-                            </select>
-                          </div>
-                          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, marginTop: 4 }}>
-                            <button className="btn btn-success" onClick={() => save(u.id)} style={{ flex: 1, justifyContent: 'center', height: 36 }}>Verify</button>
-                            <button className="btn btn-secondary" onClick={() => setEditId(null)} style={{ flex: 1, justifyContent: 'center', height: 36 }}>Batal</button>
-                          </div>
+                  </div>
+
+                  <div className="input-group">
+                    <label className="input-label">Cek Unit di Aplikasi (TEMON / GEOTAB / SMATRACK) *</label>
+                    <div className="teknisi-btn-group">
+                      {['OK', 'NOT OK'].map(o => (
+                        <button type="button" key={o} className={`teknisi-btn-option ${itCekAplikasi === o ? (o === 'OK' ? 'active' : 'active danger') : ''}`} onClick={() => setItCekAplikasi(o)}>
+                          {o}
+                        </button>
+                      ))}
+                    </div>
+                  </div>
+                </div>
+
+                <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 16 }}>
+                  <div className="photo-grid" style={{ gridTemplateColumns: '1fr', gap: 12 }}>
+                    <div className="photo-card" style={{ height: 130, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', border: '2px dashed var(--border-color)', borderRadius: 8, background: 'var(--bg-primary)' }}>
+                      {itFotoIntegrasi ? (
+                        <div style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', position: 'relative', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
+                          <a href={itFotoIntegrasi} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: '100%', height: '100%', textDecoration: 'none', background: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.08)', borderRadius: 6, color: '#60A5FA' }}>
+                            <i className="bi bi-link-45deg" style={{ fontSize: 24, marginBottom: 4 }}></i>
+                            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, textTransform: 'uppercase' }}>LIHAT FOTO INTEGRASI</span>
+                          </a>
+                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" style={{ position: 'absolute', bottom: 8, right: 8, color: '#EF4444', border: 'none', background: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.2)' }} onClick={() => setItFotoIntegrasi('')}>Hapus</button>
                         </div>
                       ) : (
-                        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
-                          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 4 }}>
-                            <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>
-                              Sistem: <Badge val={u.statusSystem} />
-                            </div>
-                            <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-secondary)' }}>
-                              Suspend: <Badge val={u.statusSuspend} />
-                            </div>
-                          </div>
-                          <button className="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onClick={() => { setEditId(u.id); setEditData({ statusSystem: u.statusSystem, statusSuspend: u.statusSuspend }); }} style={{ height: 36 }}>
-                            <i className="ti ti-shield-check"></i> Verifikasi
+                        <label style={{ cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>
+                          <i className="bi bi-camera" style={{ fontSize: 24, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', marginBottom: 4, display: 'block' }}></i>
+                          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: '#FFF' }}>Foto Integrasi Data GPS *</span>
+                          <input type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" style={{ display: 'none' }} onChange={e => handlePhotoChange('itFotoIntegrasi', e.target.files[0])} />
+                        </label>
+                      )}
+                    </div>
+
+                    <div className="photo-card" style={{ height: 130, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', border: '2px dashed var(--border-color)', borderRadius: 8, background: 'var(--bg-primary)' }}>
+                      {itFotoAbnormality ? (
+                        <div style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', position: 'relative', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
+                          <a href={itFotoAbnormality} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: '100%', height: '100%', textDecoration: 'none', background: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.08)', borderRadius: 6, color: '#60A5FA' }}>
+                            <i className="bi bi-link-45deg" style={{ fontSize: 24, marginBottom: 4 }}></i>
+                            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, textTransform: 'uppercase' }}>LIHAT FOTO ABNORMALITY</span>
+                          </a>
+                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" style={{ position: 'absolute', bottom: 8, right: 8, color: '#EF4444', border: 'none', background: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.2)' }} onClick={() => setItFotoAbnormality('')}>Hapus</button>
+                        </div>
+                      ) : (
+                        <label style={{ cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'center', padding: 10 }}>
+                          <i className="bi bi-camera" style={{ fontSize: 24, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', marginBottom: 4, display: 'block' }}></i>
+                          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: '#FFF' }}>Foto Integrasi Abnormality *</span>
+                          <input type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" style={{ display: 'none' }} onChange={e => handlePhotoChange('itFotoAbnormality', e.target.files[0])} />
+                        </label>
+                      )}
+                    </div>
+                  </div>
+
+                  <div style={{ marginTop: 'auto', display: 'flex', gap: 10, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
+                    <button className="btn btn-secondary" style={{ flex: 1, justifyContent: 'center' }} onClick={() => setEditId(null)}>Batal</button>
+                    <button className="btn btn-secondary" style={{ flex: 1, justifyContent: 'center', borderColor: '#F59E0B', color: '#F59E0B' }} onClick={saveDraft} disabled={loadingDraft}>
+                      <i className="bi bi-floppy" style={{ marginRight: 6 }}></i>Simpan Draft
+                    </button>
+                    <button className="btn btn-primary" style={{ flex: 1.5, justifyContent: 'center' }} disabled={loadingSubmit || !itFotoIntegrasi || !itFotoAbnormality} onClick={() => save(editingUnit.id)}>
+                      {loadingSubmit ? 'Mengirim...' : 'Kirim IT Verifikasi'}
+                    </button>
+                  </div>
+                </div>
+              </div>
+            </div>
+          )}
+        </div>
+      );
+    }
+
+    // 4c. CMT View
+    function CMTView({ units, setUnits, syncUpdate, isMobile }) {
+      const [q, setQ] = useState('');
+      const [loc, setLoc] = useState('');
+      const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
+      
+      const [editId, setEditId] = useState(null);
+      
+      // Form states
+      const [cmtCekAplikasi, setCmtCekAplikasi] = useState('OK');
+      const [cmtStatusPenyerahan, setCmtStatusPenyerahan] = useState('BELUM');
+      const [cmtFotoTerimaFisik, setCmtFotoTerimaFisik] = useState('');
+      const [cmtFotoSerahTerima, setCmtFotoSerahTerima] = useState('');
+      const [loadingSubmit, setLoadingSubmit] = useState(false);
+      const [loadingDraftCmt, setLoadingDraftCmt] = useState(false);
+
+      // Load draft when editId changes (CMT view)
+      React.useEffect(() => {
+        if (editId) {
+          try {
+            const saved = localStorage.getItem('cmt_draft_' + editId);
+            if (saved) {
+              const p = JSON.parse(saved);
+              setCmtCekAplikasi(p.cmtCekAplikasi || 'OK');
+              setCmtStatusPenyerahan(p.cmtStatusPenyerahan || 'BELUM');
+              if (p.cmtFotoTerimaFisik) setCmtFotoTerimaFisik(p.cmtFotoTerimaFisik);
+              if (p.cmtFotoSerahTerima) setCmtFotoSerahTerima(p.cmtFotoSerahTerima);
+            }
+          } catch (e) {}
+        }
+      }, [editId]);
+
+      const saveDraftCmt = () => {
+        if (!editId) return;
+        try {
+          localStorage.setItem('cmt_draft_' + editId, JSON.stringify({
+            cmtCekAplikasi, cmtStatusPenyerahan, cmtFotoTerimaFisik, cmtFotoSerahTerima
+          }));
+          globalAddToast('Draft CMT berhasil disimpan!', 'success');
+        } catch (e) {
+          globalAddToast('Gagal menyimpan draft!', 'danger');
+        }
+      };
+
+      const filtered = useMemo(() => {
+        return units.filter(u => 
+          u.statusPasang === 'IT VERIFIED' &&
+          (!q || u.nopol.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase())) &&
+          (!loc || u.location === loc)
+        );
+      }, [units, q, loc]);
+
+      const total = Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_LIMIT);
+      const slice = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_LIMIT, page * PAGE_LIMIT);
+
+      const handlePhotoChange = (fieldName, file) => {
+        if (!file) return;
+        globalAddToast('Mengompresi foto...', 'info');
+        const reader = new FileReader();
+        reader.onload = (e) => {
+          const originalBase64 = e.target.result;
+          const img = new Image();
+          img.onload = () => {
+            try {
+              const maxDim = 800;
+              let w = img.width;
+              let h = img.height;
+              if (w > maxDim || h > maxDim) {
+                if (w > h) {
+                  h = Math.round((h * maxDim) / w);
+                  w = maxDim;
+                } else {
+                  w = Math.round((w * maxDim) / h);
+                  h = maxDim;
+                }
+              }
+              const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
+              canvas.width = w;
+              canvas.height = h;
+              const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
+              ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);
+              const compressedBase64 = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.7);
+              if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoTerimaFisik') setCmtFotoTerimaFisik(compressedBase64);
+              if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoSerahTerima') setCmtFotoSerahTerima(compressedBase64);
+              globalAddToast('Foto berhasil ditambahkan!', 'success');
+            } catch (canvasErr) {
+              if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoTerimaFisik') setCmtFotoTerimaFisik(originalBase64);
+              if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoSerahTerima') setCmtFotoSerahTerima(originalBase64);
+              globalAddToast('Foto berhasil ditambahkan (tanpa kompresi)!', 'success');
+            }
+          };
+          img.onerror = () => {
+            if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoTerimaFisik') setCmtFotoTerimaFisik(originalBase64);
+            if (fieldName === 'cmtFotoSerahTerima') setCmtFotoSerahTerima(originalBase64);
+            globalAddToast('Foto berhasil ditambahkan!', 'success');
+          };
+          img.src = originalBase64;
+        };
+        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
+      };
+
+      const save = async (id) => {
+        const unit = units.find(u => u.id === id);
+        if (!cmtFotoTerimaFisik) {
+          globalAddToast('Kesalahan: Foto terima fisik GPS lama wajib diunggah!', 'danger');
+          return;
+        }
+        if (!cmtFotoSerahTerima) {
+          globalAddToast('Kesalahan: Foto dokumen serah terima GPS lama wajib diunggah!', 'danger');
+          return;
+        }
+
+        // Jika GPS lama belum diserahkan ke vendor, status tetap menunggu (bukan DONE)
+        const finalStatus = cmtStatusPenyerahan === 'SUDAH' ? 'DONE' : 'CMT PENDING';
+
+        setLoadingSubmit(true);
+        globalAddToast('Mengunggah foto verifikasi CMT ke server...', 'info');
+
+        let urlCmtFotoTerimaFisik = cmtFotoTerimaFisik;
+        let urlCmtFotoSerahTerima = cmtFotoSerahTerima;
+
+        try {
+          urlCmtFotoTerimaFisik = await uploadImageToSupabaseStorage(cmtFotoTerimaFisik, unit.nopol, 'cmtFotoTerimaFisik');
+          urlCmtFotoSerahTerima = await uploadImageToSupabaseStorage(cmtFotoSerahTerima, unit.nopol, 'cmtFotoSerahTerima');
+        } catch (e) {
+          console.warn("Upload storage gagal, menggunakan base64 fallback:", e);
+        }
+
+        const now = new Date();
+        const dd = n => String(n).padStart(2, '0');
+        const ts = `${dd(now.getDate())}-${dd(now.getMonth() + 1)}-${now.getFullYear()} ${dd(now.getHours())}:${dd(now.getMinutes())}`;
+
+        const updates = {
+          "STATUS REGISTRASI": finalStatus,
+          "CEK UNIT DI APLIKASI (TEMON /GEOTAB / SMATRACK) - CMT": cmtCekAplikasi,
+          "FOTO TERIMA FISIK GPS LAMA": urlCmtFotoTerimaFisik,
+          "FOTO BUKTI TERMINASI GPS LAMA": urlCmtFotoSerahTerima
+        };
+
+        try {
+          await syncUpdate(unit.nopol, updates);
+          setUnits(prev => prev.map(u => u.id === id ? {
+            ...u,
+            statusPasang: finalStatus,
+            cmtCekAplikasi,
+            cmtFotoTerimaFisik: urlCmtFotoTerimaFisik,
+            cmtFotoTerminasi: urlCmtFotoSerahTerima,
+            updatedAt: ts
+          } : u));
+          setEditId(null);
+          setCmtFotoTerimaFisik('');
+          setCmtFotoSerahTerima('');
+          try { localStorage.removeItem('cmt_draft_' + id); } catch(e) {}
+          if (finalStatus === 'DONE') {
+            globalAddToast(`Verifikasi CMT NOPOL ${unit.nopol} berhasil diselesaikan! Migrasi Lengkap.`, 'success');
+          } else {
+            globalAddToast(`CMT NOPOL ${unit.nopol} tersimpan — menunggu penyerahan GPS lama ke vendor.`, 'warning');
+          }
+        } catch (err) {
+          console.error(err);
+        } finally {
+          setLoadingSubmit(false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const editingUnit = units.find(u => u.id === editId);
+
+      return (
+        <div className="fade-in">
+          <div className="role-banner cmt">
+            <i className="bi bi-check-circle"></i>
+            <span><strong>Role: CMT</strong> — Verifikasi final penerimaan fisik GPS lama, terminasi sistem GPS lama, dan penutupan migrasi GPS.</span>
+          </div>
+
+          {!editId ? (
+            <>
+              <FilterRow>
+                <div className="search-input-wrapper">
+                  <i className="bi bi-search"></i>
+                  <input type="text" value={q} onChange={e => { setQ(e.target.value); setPage(1); }} className="search-input" placeholder="Cari NOPOL..." />
+                </div>
+                <select value={loc} onChange={e => { setLoc(e.target.value); setPage(1); }} className="filter-select">
+                  <option value="">Semua Lokasi</option>
+                  {LOCS.map(l => <option key={l} value={l}>{l}</option>)}
+                </select>
+                <span className="unit-count-tag">{filtered.length} Unit Menunggu CMT</span>
+              </FilterRow>
+
+              {filtered.length === 0 ? (
+                <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 48, color: 'var(--text-tertiary)', background: 'var(--bg-card)', borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)', border: '1px solid var(--border-color)', marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  <i className="bi bi-list-check" style={{ fontSize: 32, display: 'block', marginBottom: 10, color: 'var(--text-tertiary)' }}></i>
+                  Tidak ada unit berstatus IT VERIFIED yang membutuhkan verifikasi final CMT.
+                </div>
+              ) : isMobile ? (
+                <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 12, marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  {slice.map(u => (
+                    <div key={u.id} className="mobile-unit-card" style={{ padding: 14 }}>
+                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
+                        <strong style={{ fontSize: 15 }}>{u.nopol}</strong>
+                        <Badge val={u.statusPasang} />
+                      </div>
+                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-secondary)', marginTop: 6 }}>
+                        <div>Site: {u.location} • Pool: {u.pool}</div>
+                        <div>IT Verified By: <strong>IT Team</strong></div>
+                      </div>
+                      <button className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" style={{ width: '100%', marginTop: 12, justifyContent: 'center' }} onClick={() => { setEditId(u.id); setCmtCekAplikasi('OK'); setCmtStatusPenyerahan('BELUM'); setCmtFotoTerimaFisik(''); setCmtFotoSerahTerima(''); }}>
+                        <i className="bi bi-clipboard-check"></i> Mulai Verifikasi Final
+                      </button>
+                    </div>
+                  ))}
+                </div>
+              ) : (
+                <div className="table-container" style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
+                  <table className="data-table">
+                    <thead>
+                      <tr>
+                        <th>#</th>
+                        <th>NOPOL</th>
+                        <th>LOCATION</th>
+                        <th>POOL</th>
+                        <th>TEKNISI</th>
+                        <th>PIC</th>
+                        <th>IT STATUS</th>
+                        <th>AKSI</th>
+                      </tr>
+                    </thead>
+                    <tbody>
+                      {slice.map((u, i) => (

+// Helper untuk mencari atau membuat folder "image GPS"
+function getOrCreateImageFolder(ss) {
+  var fileId = ss.getId();
+  var file = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
+  var parents = file.getParents();
+  var parentFolder = null;
+  if (parents.hasNext()) {
+    parentFolder = parents.next();
+  } else {
+    parentFolder = DriveApp.getRootFolder();
+  }
+  
+  var folderName = "image GPS";
+  var folders = parentFolder.getFoldersByName(folderName);
+  if (folders.hasNext()) {
+    return folders.next();
+  } else {
+    var newFolder = parentFolder.createFolder(folderName);
+    return newFolder;
+  }
+}
